 yah ‘edwocket on ricard’ mukademe kii sunwaayee ke samay ek baar bhi upasthit nahin hua
 Advocates on record are lawyers who are eligible to petition in the apex court
 iske liye sheersh adaalat baqayada pariksha letaa he
 The Court held that Advocate on Record is not a 'guest artist' who merely signs the petition
 nyaayalay ne kaha ki is tarah kaa ravaiya to bholebhaale vaadiyon ke prati bahut hi krurtapurna he or edwocket on record kaa aisa aacharan edwocket on record ke anuroop nahin he
 The court said that a lawyer willfully ignoring the interests of the litigant is not consistent with a lawyer
 nyaayalay ne kaha ki kanoon vyapaar nahin he
 a lawyer is an officer of the court and hence it is his duty to ensure the functioning of the court in a smooth manner
 vakil ko sankat main ghire vyakti kii ummide jagaani hoti hai or vah asahaay vaadi kaa shoshan nahin kar saktaa he

 ) brazil ke ek chikitsak par aspataal kii shaiya khaali karaane ke liye saat marijon kii hatya karne kaa andeh he
 The incident in southern Brazil is being investigated for killing 300 other patients
 yah jaankaree jaanchakartaaon ne di
 a team led by Health Ministry investigator Mario Lobato has been investigating 1,872 deaths during the last seven years in the intensive care unit supervised by Virginia Soars at Evangelico Hospital in the city of Coritiba in South Paraná province, Xinhua reported
 sarkari abhiyojkon ke mutabik soars or uski chikitsa team ne ikai main bhartee marijon kii peshiyon ko shithil karne vaali dawa di or unki oxigen aapurti kam kar di jisase shwaas main avrodh paidaa hua
 Prosecutors have said that this was revealed by telephone tapping in which they found that Soars killed patients to empty the unit's beds
 56 varshiya vidhwaa chikitsak teen anya chikitsakon or teen nurson or ek fijiotherapist ke saath farvari main giraftaar kii gai thi
 All have been charged with seven murders
 tippaniyan On Sunday, Lobato told Brazil's Globo TV that 20 deaths looked suspicious and another 300 deaths were being investigated
 sabhi main peshi dhili karne or oxigen kii kami ke lakshan paae gaye hai
 If prosecutors prove that Soars killed 300 patients, it would be considered the world's most horrific serial murder
 giraftaar ke samay soars ne aaropon se inkaar kiya tha

 abhiyojkon ne kaha he ki is baat kaa khulaasa telephone tanping se hua jisamen unhone paaya ki soars ne ikai ke bistaron ko khaali karne ke liye marijon kii hatya kii he
 The 56-year-old widow was arrested in February along with three other physicians and three nurses and a physiotherapist
 sabhi ko saat hatyaon kaa aaropee banaaya gaya he
 The comments ravivaar ko lobato ne brazil ke globo tivi ko bataaya ki 20 mautein sandigdh lag rahi hai or anya 300 mauton kii jaanch kii ja rahi he
 Signs of muscle loss and oxygen deficiency have been found in all
 yadi abhiyojak sabit kar dete hai ki soars ne 300 rogiyon kii hatya kii he to yah duniya kaa sabase bhishantam shrinkhalabaddh hatya mana jayega

 Deepa is now busy with the final preparations
 unke pita tathaa bhartiya khel praadhikaran (sai) main bharottolan ke coach or unki mata mangalvaar ko ek khaas puja karenge
 Deepa will turn 23 on Tuesday and this special puja is being organized to win her
 sai ke coach or deepa ke pita dulaal karmkaar ne ieenes ko bataaya, "olympic ke final main deepa ke pahunchane kii khushkhabari na keval ham sab khush hai, balki har bhartiya jashn manaa rahaa he

 " Deepa was awarded the Arjuna Award last year

 a post shared by Katrina Kaif (@katrinakaif) on Mar 31, 2018 at 6:56 am PDT a post shared by Isabelle Kaif (@isakaif) on Mar 31, 2018 at 9:11 am PDTA post shared by Deepika Padukone (@deepikapadukone) on Feb 2, 2018 at 9:13 am PSTA post shared by Anisha Padukone (@anishapadukone) on Feb 2, 2018 at 5:41 am PSTA post shared by Nupur Sanon (@nupursanon) on Mar 23, 2018 at 9:19 am PDTA post shared by Nupur Sanon (@nupursanon) on Mar 29, 2018 at 6:14 am PDTA post shared by Shaheen Bhatt (@shaheenb) on Mar 14, 2018 at 8:06 pm pdti've lived with depression on and off since i was about 13 years old 
 This is not a revelation or a confession
 Those who know me know this about me
 It's not something i take any pains to hide, I'm not ashamed of it or particularly troubled by it
 It's just a part of who i am
 i have days where i feel good and then i have days where i don't
 One minute everything's fine and the next it's like someone turned the light off inside my head
 i go quiet and it's difficult to get out of bed
 Like it always does the world around me loses focus and i struggle to make sense of it
 Sometimes these bouts last an hour - sometimes they last days
 Today, I'm on day 4
 i say i live with depression rather than i struggle with it because for me (and i speak only for myself here) i don't see why it has to be a struggle
 i once read an idea by an American essayist called Richard Mitchell which stayed with me; it's now become how i try to approach the dips in my week or month
 The idea is this: To be sick, or to suffer, is inevitable
 But to become bitter and vindictive in sickness and suffering and to surrender to irrationality, supposing yourself the innocent and virtuous victim of the evils intentions of the world, is not inevitable
 The appropriate answer to the question - Why me? is the other question - Why not me? *** Why am i writing about this? Well, i spend a fair amount of time on social media during the course of my day and today i found myself looking for something to post because it's been a few days since I've posted anything
 i couldn't find anything so i figured I'd just talk about this - how I'm doing, instead of what I'm doing
 It's as simple as that, and we could all stand to do a little more of it
 P

 45 to 9
 45 baje ke bich vikram lander chandrayan-2 ke orbitor kaa peechha chhod nai kaksha main jayega
 Then it will circle the moon at 109 km apogee and 120 km perigee
 ise vaigyanik bhashaa main diorbit kehete hai yani jis disha main vah ja rahaa tha, uske vipareet disha main aage badhanaa
 After separation from the orbiter, the Vikram lander will rotate around the moon in the opposite direction of the orbiter at a speed of 2 km per second
 aisa isliye kiya rahaa hai kyonki orbitor chand ke chaaron taraf upar 100 kimi kii duuri par chakkar lagayegaa
 But, Vikram Lander has to change his direction to get to the south pole of the moon
 isliye use vipareet disha main chand kaa chakkar lagaana hoga
 On September 4, Vikram will change for the second time around the moon, bringing his orbiter scientist Vikram Lander to the nearest orbit of the moon between 3 to 4 pm on 4 September
 is kaksha kii apoji 36 kimi or periji 110 kimi hogi

 pragyan rover ke sehat kii bhi jaanch kii jaaegi
 September 7 will be the most challenging, Vikram Lander will land on the moon 1: 30 to 1

 yah isro vaigyanikon ke liye behad chunauteepurn kaam hoga

 saath hi isro se bheje gaye cmand ko lander or rover tak pahunchayegaa

 It has 4 payloads
 yah 15 dinon tak vaigyanik prayog karegaa

 baad main ise bengalooru ke yuaressi ne viksit kiya

 isamen 2 pelod hai

 is puri prakriya main kareeb 15 minute lagenge
